\DoxyCodeLine{    ACPI\_COMMENT\_NODE               *CommentList;       \textcolor{comment}{/* comments that appears before this node */}\(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{    ACPI\_COMMENT\_NODE               *EndBlkComment;     \textcolor{comment}{/* comments that at the end of a block but before ) or \} */}\(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{    char                            *CvFilename;        \textcolor{comment}{/* Filename associated with this node. Used for ASL/ASL+ converter */}\(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{    char                            *CvParentFilename)  \textcolor{comment}{/* Parent filename associated with this node. Used for ASL/ASL+ converter */}}

\end{DoxyCode}
